Chrome can note topics of interest based on your recent browsing history. Later, a site you visit can ask Chrome for relevant topics to personalize the ads you see.You can make changes in ad privacy settings<b>What data is used?</b> Your ad topics are based on your recent browsing history, a list of sites you've visited using Chrome on this device.<b>How do sites use this data?</b> Chrome notes topics of interest as you browse. Topic labels are predefined and include things like, Arts & Entertainment, Shopping, and Sports. Later, a site you visit can ask Chrome for a few of your topics to personalize the ads you see.Google requires companies to state publicly that they won't use this data to track you across sites. Any effect depends on whether a website responds to the request, and how the request is interpreted. For example, some websites may respond to this request by showing you ads that aren't based on other websites you've visited.
